<h1 _ngcontent-rod-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.UiTest"> @ohos.UiTest </h1>

<div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>UiTest提供模拟UI操作的能力，供开发者在测试场景使用，主要支持如点击、双击、长按、滑动等UI操作能力。</p>    <p>该模块提供以下功能：</p>    <ul>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#on9">On<sup>9+</sup></a>：提供控件特征描述能力，用于控件筛选匹配查找。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#component9">Component<sup>9+</sup></a>：代表UI界面上的指定控件，提供控件属性获取，控件点击，滑动查找，文本注入等能力。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#driver9">Driver<sup>9+</sup></a>：入口类，提供控件匹配/查找，按键注入，坐标点击/滑动，截图等能力。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#uiwindow9">UiWindow<sup>9+</sup></a>：入口类，提供窗口属性获取，窗口拖动、调整窗口大小等能力。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#bydeprecated">By<sup>(deprecated)</sup></a>：提供控件特征描述能力，用于控件筛选匹配查找。从API version 9开始不再维护，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#on9">On<sup>9+</sup></a>。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#uicomponentdeprecated">UiComponent<sup>(deprecated)</sup></a>：代表UI界面上的指定控件，提供控件属性获取，控件点击，滑动查找，文本注入等能力。从API version 9开始不再维护，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#component9">Component<sup>9+</sup></a>。</li>     <li><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#uidriverdeprecated">UiDriver<sup>(deprecated)</sup></a>：入口类，提供控件匹配/查找，按键注入，坐标点击/滑动，截图等能力。从API version 9开始不再维护，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#driver9">Driver<sup>9+</sup></a>。</li>    </ul>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>本模块首批接口从API version 8开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</li>       <li>本模块接口在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/uitest-guidelines" target="_blank">自动化测试脚本</a>中使用。</li>       <li>本模块接口不支持并发调用。</li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">WindowMode<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 834px;">     <h2 id="inputtextmode20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">InputTextMode<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.5.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.5.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" <p>输入文本时是否指定以复制粘贴方式输入。true：指定以复制粘贴方式输入。false：指定以逐字键入方式输入。默认为false。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong> 当输入文本中包含中文、特殊字符或文本长度超过200字符时，无论该参数取值为何，均以复制粘贴方式输入。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 583px;">     <h2 id="on9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">On<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="on9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>UiTest框架从API version 9开始，通过On类提供了丰富的控件特征描述API，用于进行控件筛选来匹配/查找出目标控件。</p>     <p>On提供的API能力具有以下几个特点:</p>     <p>1、支持单属性匹配和多属性组合匹配，例如同时指定目标控件text和id。</p>     <p>2、控件属性支持多种匹配模式。</p>     <p>3、支持控件绝对定位，相对定位，可通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#isbefore9">ON.isBefore</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#isafter9">ON.isAfter</a>等API限定邻近控件特征进行辅助定位。</p>     <p>On类提供的所有API均为同步接口，建议使用者通过静态构造器ON来链式创建On对象。</p>     <div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-variable constant_">ON</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.TestKit'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-variable constant_">ON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">text</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'123'</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">type</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'Button'</span>);</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1357px;">     <h3 id="text9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">text<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="text9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>text(txt: string, pattern?: MatchPattern): On</p>     <p>指定目标控件文本属性，支持多种匹配模式，返回On对象自身。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>如果控件的无障碍属性<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-accessibility#accessibilitylevel">accessibilityLevel</a>设置为'no'或'no-hide-descendants'，无法使用本接口指定目标控件的文本属性用于查找控件，可以使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#originaltext20">On.originalText()</a>接口实现。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">txt</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1212px;">     <h3 id="checkable9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">checkable<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#on9">On</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回指定控件所属屏幕的On对象。</td>        </tr> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1325px;">     <h3 id="originaltext20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">originalText<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="originaltext20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>originalText(text: string, pattern?: MatchPattern): On</p>     <p>指定控件的文本内容和文本匹配模式，返回On对象自身。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>如果控件的无障碍属性<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-accessibility#accessibilitylevel">accessibilityLevel</a>设置为'no'或'no-hide-descendants'，可以使用本接口指定目标控件的文本属性用于查找控件，使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#text9">On.text()</a>接口不生效。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.39.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">text</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定控件文本，用于匹配目标控件文本。 可以借助<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/deveco-testing" target="_blank">DevEco Testing</a>中UiViewer获取控件节点属性。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">pattern</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#matchpattern">MatchPattern</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的文本匹配模式，默认为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#matchpattern">EQUALS</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#on9">On</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回指定目标控件文本属性的On对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 230px;">     <h2 id="component9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Component<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="component9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>UiTest框架在API9中，Component类代表了UI界面上的一个控件，提供控件属性获取，控件点击，滑动查找，文本注入等API。</p>     <p>该类提供的所有方法都使用Promise方式作为异步方法，需使用await调用。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1052px;">     <h3 id="click9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#getoriginaltext20">Component.getOriginalText()</a>获取控件的文本信息。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputText<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>inputText(text: string, mode: InputTextMode): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>向控件中输入文本，并支持指定文本输入方式，仅针对可编辑的文本组件生效，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">输入的文本信息，当前支持英文、中文和特殊字符。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>输入文本的方式，取值请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#inputtextmode20">InputTextMode</a>。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong> InputTextMode.addition取值为ture时，在控件已有文本末尾后追加指定文本。取值为false时，指定文本将覆盖控件已有文本。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。无返回结果的Promise对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">scrollSearch<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="scrollsearch18" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>scrollSearch(on: On, vertical?: boolean, offset?: number): Promise&lt;Component&gt;</p>     <p>在控件上滑动查找目标控件（适用支持滑动的控件），支持指定滑动方向和滑动起止点与组件边框的偏移量，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.61.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">on</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#on9">On</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">目标控件的属性要求。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">vertical</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">默认为true，表示查找方向是纵向。false表示查找方向为横向。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">offset</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">滑动起点/终点到组件边框的偏移，默认80，单位：px，取值范围：大于等于0的整数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#component9">Component</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象，返回目标控件对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Driver<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Driver类为uitest测试框架的总入口，提供控件匹配/查找，按键注入，坐标点击/滑动，截图等能力。</p>     <p>该类提供的方法除Driver.create()以外的所有方法都使用Promise方式作为异步方法，需使用await方式调用。</p>    </div>    <div <h3 id="triggercombinekeys20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">triggerCombineKeys<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>triggerCombineKeys(key0: number, key1: number, key2?: number, displayId?: number): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>通过给定的key值，找到对应组合键，并在指定屏幕下进行点击，使用Promise异步回调。例如，Key值为(2072, 2019)时，找到key值对应的组合键并点击，如Ctrl+c。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> width="25%">以number的形式传入目的点的纵坐标信息，取值范围：大于等于0的整数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">speed</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">滑动速率，取值范围为200-40000的整数，默认值为600，不在范围内设为默认值为600，单位：px/s。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。无返回结果的Promise对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1690px;">     <h3 id="dragbetween20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">dragBetween<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="dragbetween20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>dragBetween(from: Point, to: Point, speed?: number, duration?: number): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>从起始坐标点拖拽至目标坐标点，支持指定拖拽速度和拖拽前长按时间，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异</strong>：该接口在Phone、Tablet、PC/2in1、TV设备上生效，在其他设备中调用无效果。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.94.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.94.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.94.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.94.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">from</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#point9">Point</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">以Point对象的形式传入起始点的坐标信息和所属屏幕ID。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">to</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#point9">Point</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>以Point对象的形式传入终止点的坐标信息和所属屏幕ID。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong> 应与起始点属于同一个屏幕，否则将抛出17000007异常。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">speed</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">滑动速率，取值范围为200-40000的整数，默认值为600，不在范围内设为默认值为600，单位：px/s。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">duration</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">拖拽前长按持续的时间，取值范围为大于等于1500的整数，默认值为1500，单位：ms。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#point9">Point</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象，返回Point对象，当前设备指定屏幕的大小为Point.x * Point.y。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1456px;">     <h3 id="screencapture10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">screenCapture<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="screencapture10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>screenCapture(savePath: string, rect?: Rect): Promise&lt;boolean&gt;</p>     <p>捕获当前屏幕的指定区域，并保存为PNG格式的图片至给出的保存路径中，使用Promise异步回调。适用于支持截屏的场景。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.113.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.113.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.113.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.113.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">savePath</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文件保存路径。路径需为当前应用的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/app-sandbox-directory" target="_blank">沙箱路径</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">rect</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#rect9">Rect</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">截图区域，默认为全屏。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.113.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.113.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;boolean&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象，返回截图操作是否成功完成。true：成功完成，false：未成功完成。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">mouseClick<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="mouseclick10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>mouseClick(p: Point, btnId: MouseButton, key1?: number, key2?: number): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>在指定坐标点注入鼠标点击动作，支持同时按下对应键盘组合键，使用Promise异步回调。例如，Key值为2072时，按下Ctrl并进行鼠标点击动作。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="mousescroll11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>在指定坐标点注入鼠标滚轮滑动动作，支持同时按下对应键盘组合键并且指定滑动速度，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th  </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">down</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">滚轮滑动方向是否向下。true表示向下滑动。false表示向上滚动。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">d</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">key1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span <p>在指定坐标点注入鼠标长按动作，支持同时按下对应键盘组合键，使用Promise异步回调。例如，Key值为2072时，按下Ctrl并进行鼠标长按动作。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1453px;">     <h3 id="mousedrag11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">mouseDrag<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="mousedrag11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>mouseDrag(from: Point, to: Point, speed?: number): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>鼠标按住鼠标左键从起始坐标点拖拽至终点坐标点，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异</strong>：该接口在Phone、Tablet、PC/2in1、TV设备上生效，在其他设备中调用无效果。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1360px;">     <h3 id="inputtext11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputText<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>inputText(p: Point, text: string): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>在指定坐标点输入文本，不清空组件内原有文本，直接在坐标处追加输入，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputText<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>inputText(p: Point, text: string, mode: InputTextMode): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>在指定坐标点输入文本，支持指定文本输入方式，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#point9">Point</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">输入文本的坐标点。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">text</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">输入的文本信息，当前支持英文、中文和特殊字符。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#inputtextmode20">InputTextMode</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>输入文本的方式，取值请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#inputtextmode20">InputTextMode</a>。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>InputTextMode.addition取值为ture时，将光标移动至文本末尾后输入指定文本。取值为false时，将在坐标点位置输入指定文本。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">crownRotate<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="crownrotate20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>crownRotate(d: number, speed?: number): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>注入手表表冠旋转事件，可指定旋转速度，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异</strong>：该接口在Wearable设备中可正常调用，在其他设备中返回801错误码。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.133.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">speed</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="uiwindow9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>UiWindow代表了UI界面上的一个窗口，提供窗口属性获取，窗口拖动、调整窗口大小等能力。</p>     <p>该类提供的所有方法都使用Promise方式作为异步方法，需使用await方式调用。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1052px;">     <h3 id="getbundlename9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">getBundleName<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getbundlename9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getBundleName(): Promise&lt;string&gt;</p>     <p>获取窗口归属应用的包名信息，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p> width="50%">Promise&lt;string&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象，返回窗口归属应用的包名信息。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">isFocused<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>isFocused(): Promise&lt;boolean&gt;</p>     <p>判断窗口是否处于获焦状态，使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;boolean&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象，返回窗口对象是否获取获焦状态。true：获焦。false：未获焦。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">resize<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="resize9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>resize(wide: number, height: number, direction: ResizeDirection): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>根据传入的宽、高和调整方向来调整窗口的大小，使用Promise异步回调。适用于支持调整大小的窗口。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Test.UiTest</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.146.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.146.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.146.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.146.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">wide</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">以number的形式传入调整后窗口的宽度，取值范围：大于等于0的整数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">height</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">以number的形式传入调整后窗口的高度，取值范围：大于等于0的整数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">direction</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#resizedirection9">ResizeDirection</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">以<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#resizedirection9">ResizeDirection</a>的形式传入窗口调整的方向。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="oncedialogshow10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 631px;">     <h2 id="bydeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">By<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bydeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>UiTest框架通过By类提供了丰富的控件特征描述API，用于进行控件筛选来匹配/查找出目标控件。</p>     <p>By提供的API能力具有以下几个特点:</p>     <p>1、支持单属性匹配和多属性组合匹配，例如同时指定目标控件text和id。</p>     <p>2、控件属性支持多种匹配模式。</p>     <p>3、支持控件绝对定位，相对定位，可通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#isbeforedeprecated">By.isBefore<sup>(deprecated)</sup></a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#isafterdeprecated">By.isAfter<sup>(deprecated)</sup></a>等API限定邻近控件特征进行辅助定位。</p>     <p>By类提供的所有API均为同步接口，建议使用者通过静态构造器BY来链式创建By对象。</p>     <p>从API version 9开始不再维护，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-uitest#on9">On<sup>9+</sup></a>。</p>     <div _ngcontent-rod-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">UiDriver<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>UiDriver类为uitest测试框架的总入口，提供控件匹配/查找，按键注入，坐标点击/滑动，截图等API。</p>     <p>该类提供的方法除UiDriver.create()以外的所有方法都使用Promise方式作为异步方法，需使用await调用。</p>     <p>从API
